Chang's China Bistro, Inc. ===\n[[Image:PF_Changs_Maryland.jpg|thumb|300px|right|P.F. Chang's at The Mall in Columbia in Columbia, Maryland]]\nP. F. Chang's China Bistro, Inc. is an American restaurant chain founded in Scottsdale, Arizona in 1993 by Paul Fleming. The restaurants serve American [[Chinese cuisine]] from a menu originally conceived and planned by chef Philip Chiang. P. F. Chang's is the namesake of Paul Fleming (P. F.) and Philip Chiang (whose surname is simplified to Chang.)\n\nP. F. Chang's operates exclusively in the United States; As of December 2005, PFCCB Administration, Inc. maintains 133 restaurants in 34 states. P.F. Chang's corporate headquarters is in Phoenix, Arizona.\n\nP. F. Chang's is one of a few restaurant chains that offers a dedicated menu to diners that must follow a strict [[gluten]]-free diet.\n====Trivia====\nThe restaurant chain is frequently referenced in the animated sitcom South Park. Laura Cherry, a spokesperson for the chain, has spoken positively of the series, and stated that creators Trey Parker and Matt Stone frequently dine there.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n{{RecipeSkip}}\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:12032020'>#pfchangschinabistrorecipes #gluten #chinesecuisine #orientalcuisine #recipes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

#pansearedsalmonsteakswithcucumbergingerandgarlic #garlic #sesameoil #limejuice #fishsauce #salmonsteaks #lime #marinade #seeds #foodprocessor \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This Chinese recipe is a completely different way to use cucumbers with salmon\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1126\n|PortionCalories = 563\n|DatePublished=21st January |TotalTime = 1 hour 10 minutes plus\n |PrepTime = 1 hour plus\n |CookTime = 10 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Pan seared salmon steaks with cucumber, ginger and garlic recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">A lovely light meal</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nIf you grow your own [[Cucumbers|cucumbers]] you'll know that you tend to get a glut of them when they are in season and are probably always seeking new [[Cucumber|cucumber]] recipe ideas, this one is a unique and exotic way of using up another cucumber.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 cm (1.5\" fresh [[Root ginger|root ginger]], peeled and chopped)\n| 2 [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves, peeled and chopped\n| 2 [[Indian green chillies]], de-seeded\n| 3 tablespoons [[Jaggery|jaggery]] or [[Brown sugar|brown sugar]]\n| 3 tablespoons [[Fish sauce|fish sauce]] ([[Nuoc mam|nuoc mam]] or [[Nam pla|nam pla]])\n| [[Juice]] from 1 [[Lime|lime]] or 2-3 tablespoons [[Lime juice|lime juice]]\n| 4 tablespoons of water\n| 1 small [[Cucumber|cucumber]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Sesame oil|sesame oil]]\n| 4 [[Salmon steaks|Salmon steaks]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Using a [[Pestle and mortar|pestle and mortar]], [[Food processor|food processor]] or mini-chopper, grind the [[Sugar|sugar]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Ginger|ginger]] and [[Chillies|chillies]] to a pulp.\n| Mix in the [[Fish sauce|fish sauce]], water and [[Lime juice|lime juice]]\n| Add the dressing to the fish and [[marinade]] for an hour or so.\n| Cut the [[Cucumber|cucumber]] into quarters lengthwise and run a knife down each quadrant to remove the [[Seeds|seeds]]\n| Using a [[Speed-peeler|speed-peeler]] or [[Mandoline|mandoline]] cut the [[Cucumber|cucumber]] into long thin strips.\n| Remove the fish from the marinade and replace with the cucumber strips and marinade for no more than 10 minutes or they start to loose their crunch.\n| Rub the [[Sesame oil|sesame oil]] on the [[Grill pan|grill pan]] and pan [[Sear|sear]] the [[salmon steaks|salmon steaks]] for a few minutes on each side.\n| Remove from the heat and rest, covered for 5 minutes.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nGarnish with the [[Cucumber|cucumber]] strips, pour over the dressing and serve. \n===Variations===\n[[Chopped spring onions|chopped spring onions]] go nicely with this.\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental This one uses tuna steaks\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1006\n|PortionCalories = 503\n|DatePublished=21st January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Served with chilled rice timbales spring onions\n |Servings = Serves 2 to 4 - use the same ingredient quantities, just increase the amount of fish\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 10 minutes plus\n |PrepTime = 1 hour plus\n |CookTime = 10 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Pan seared tuna with cucumber, ginger and garlic recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Michelin star stuff!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Looked and tasted fab.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nIf you grow your own [[Cucumbers|cucumbers]] you'll know that you tend to get a glut of them when they are in season and are probably always seeking new [[Cucumber|cucumber]] recipe ideas, this one is a unique and exotic way of using up another cucumber.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 cm (1.5\" fresh [[Root ginger|root ginger]], peeled and chopped)\n| 2 [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves, peeled and chopped\n| 2 [[Indian green chillies]], de-seeded\n| 3 tablespoons [[Jaggery|jaggery]] or [[Brown sugar|brown sugar]]\n| 3 tablespoons [[Fish sauce|fish sauce]] ([[Nuoc mam|nuoc mam]] or [[Nam pla|nam pla]])\n| [[Juice]] from 1 [[Lime|lime]] or 2-3 tablespoons [[Lime juice|lime juice]]\n| 4 tablespoons of water\n| 1 small [[Cucumber|cucumber]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Sesame oil|sesame oil]]\n| 4 [[Tuna steaks|tuna steaks]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Using a [[Pestle and mortar|pestle and mortar]], [[Food processor|food processor]] or mini-chopper, grind the [[Sugar|sugar]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Ginger|ginger]] and [[Chillies|chillies]] to a pulp.\n| Mix in the [[Fish sauce|fish sauce]], water and [[Lime juice|lime juice]].\n| Add the mixture to the fish and marinade for an hour or so.\n| Cut the [[Cucumber|cucumber]] into quarters lengthwise and run a knife down each quadrant to remove the [[Seeds|seeds]]\n| Using a [[Speed-peeler|speed-peeler]] or [[Mandoline|mandoline]] cut the [[Cucumber|cucumber]] into long thin strips.\n| Remove the fish from the marinade and add the cucumber strips to the dressing and [[Marinade|marinade]] for no more than 10 minutes or they start to loose their crunch.\n| Rub the [[Sesame oil|sesame oil]] on the [[Grill pan|grill pan]] and pan [[Sear|sear]] the [[Tuna steaks|tuna steaks]] for a few minutes on each side.\n| Remove from the heat and rest, covered for 5 minutes.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nGarnish with the [[Cucumber|cucumber]] strips, pour over the dressing and serve with cold rice moulds (timbales) and a few chopped spring onions.  Eating the long lengths of cucumber was quite fun, rolling up on a fork like spaghetti.\n===Variations===\nI always use my [[homemade lazy ginger]] instead of fresh ginger as it keeps so much better and tastes as good.  Instead of the water, I used the lovely gingery vinegar from my [[lazy ginger]].\n===Chef's notes===\nA fabulous recipe this, the only change I would make would be to slice the cucumber a little thicker using a [[mandoline]] instead of a [[speed peeler]].\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Vietnamese recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#cucumber #mandoline #pansearedtunasteakswithcucumbergingerandgarlic #sesameoil #garlic #tunasteaks #fishsauce #limejuice #panfried #nuocmam #cucumbers </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Peking duck",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Peking duck, Meat recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#pekingduck #cucumber #duck #lemon #crispyduckpancakes #julienned #springonions #teatowel #bakedorroastedduck #cochinitapibil #vinegar \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Whilst whole, pre-prepared Peking duck (also known as aromatic duck) can be bought from some supermarkets and Chinese wholesalers\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 4001\n|PortionCalories = 1000\n|DatePublished=18th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 3\n|TotalTime = 1 hour 5 minutes plus overnight\n|PrepTime = 15 minutes\n|CookTime = 50 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Peking duck recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">No bicycle pump required</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Even though I love my cookery, pre-prepared is the way to go.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nWhilst whole, pre-prepared Peking duck (also known as aromatic duck) can be bought from some supermarkets and Chinese wholesalers such as [http://www.seewoo.com Seewoo], it's quite fun to prepare one from scratch with a [[fresh duck]].  Have a go at this as it's pretty simple to do and does not involve a bicycle pump - as I saw on one TV program a few years ago!\n[[Image:Aromatic duck.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Commercially prepared aromatic duck - \u00a37.50 (2008)]]\n\nYou can make the [[crispy duck pancakes]] from our [[special crispy duck pancake recipe]] or buy them from an Asian wholesaler.  Look in the freezer compartments, they are usually sold [[frozen]] in quantities of about 100, separately wrapped in 10's.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 whole [[duck]] - plucked and oven ready\n| 6 [[spring onions]] - [[Julienned|julienned]]\n| 1 [[cucumber]], peeled, de-seeded if you're apt to wind, and julienned.\n| 1 [[lemon]]\n| 3 tablespoons [[maltose]]\n| 1 tablespoon Chinese red wine\n| 20 [[Crispy duck pancakes]] or [[lettuce]] leaves to roll in\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Set a large pan of water boiling, immerse the [[duck]] and cook for 5 minutes, stirring frequently. Take out the duck, and refresh for a minute in a large bowl of cold water\n| Allow to drip-dry, ideally by hanging from a hook or resting on a rack\n| Mix 18fl oz (500ml) boiling water with the juice and rind of 1 [[lemon]], together with 3 tablespoons maltose and 1 tablespoon Chinese red wine [[vinegar]]\n| With a clean & dry cloth or [[tea towel]], dry the duck inside and out\n| Using a pastry or [[Basting|basting brush]], paint the marinade all over\n| Hanging to dry, preferably overnight\n| In the hottest oven you can muster, roast the duck for 45 minutes\n| Remove from the oven and rest for 10 minutes\n| When carving, strip all of the meat and skin from the bird and then, using two forks, shred it to smithereens\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nIf you've had this dish before, waste no more time, just get to it and eat. \n\nOtherwise, read on: lay out each pancake as and when you are ready to eat it. Spread a teaspoon of the sauce of your choosing (hoisin, [[chili]], plum). Add a small portion of [[cucumber]]. Ditto, spring [[onions]]. Add some shredded duck, roll up and eat. Repeat until the duck is no more (it is an ex-duck!!).\n\n[[Plum & ginger sauce]] goes well with Peking duck too.\n\n===Mexican Variations===\n\nAlthough it needs easy preparation but which is 24 hours in advance, try [[Cochinita pibil]] (pork) instead of duck as the meat filling for the pancakes.\n\n===North African===\n\nOr my own North African-styled variation with lamb: [[Spicy lamb tortillas]].\n\n==See also==\n* '''Procedure to make a [[How to make crispy aromatic duck at home|complete crispy duck meal at home]].'''\n\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Duck]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes|Duck]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine|Duck]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Duck]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Duck]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted|Duck]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pekingduck #cucumber #duck #lemon #crispyduckpancakes #julienned #springonions #teatowel #bakedorroastedduck #cochinitapibil #vinegar </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  15 minutes\n|PrepTime =  10 minutes\n|CookTime =  5 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Philadelphia oriental salad recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Nice and simple</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Somethimes the best way for a salad</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Carla_Cancio-Bello,_J.D.,_on_behalf_of_Cuban_Cuisine_UK|Carla]] </span></span>\n}}\nA quick and healthy [[Salad|salad]] that is so simple it deserves to be in our [[Cookery|cookery]] [[Cheats section|cheats section]].\n\n{{PhiladelphiaPermission}}\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 150 g pack ready to cook ribbon [[Noodles|noodles]] (see Chef's notes)\n| 50 g [[Mange touts|mange touts]], halved diagonally\n| 50 g [[French beans]], halved\n| 2 [[Spring onions|spring onions]], trimmed and chopped\n| 100 g cooked tiger [[Prawns|prawns]]\n| 60 g Philadelphia Light\n| 1 tablespoon sweet [[Chilli sauce|chilli sauce]]\n| 2 teaspoons of [[Fish sauce|fish sauce]]\n| Rind and [[Juice|juice]] of \u00bd [[Lime|lime]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Semi-skimmed milk|semi-skimmed milk]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Cook the [[Noodles|noodles]] according to the pack ([[Microwave|microwave]] works well) and cool in a [[Sieve|sieve]] under cold water.\n| [[Blanch]] the [[Mangetouts|mangetouts]] and [[Beans|beans]] for 1 minute in [[Boiling|boiling]] water, drain and cool under cold water.\n| Mix the Philadelphia with the sweet [[Chilli|chilli]], [[Fish sauce|fish sauce]], [[Lime|lime]] and [[Milk|milk]].\n|Arrange [[Noodles|noodles]], [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and [[Prawns|prawns]] between serving plates and drizzle over the Philadelphia dressing.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n* [http://www.philadelphia.co.uk/philadelphia3/page?siteid=philadelphia3-prd&locale=uken1&PagecRef=609&rid=9293 The Philadelphia recipe title": "Pork Stir Fry",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Pork Stir Fry, Meat recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#porkstirfry #nuts #cashews #wok #cornflour #pork #noodles #mangetout #muscovadosugar #orange #stirfry \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=An easy recipe costing around \u00a32.50 per serving\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2797\n|PortionCalories = 699\n|DatePublished=31st October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 35 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Pork Stir Fry recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Easy Chinese at home</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">With no fancy ingredients, you can easily make this great meal at home tonight.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nAn easy recipe costing around \u00a32.50 per serving. Best prepared using higher-welfare [[Pork|pork]], labelled as Freedom Food, outdoor reared, outdoor bred, free-range or organic. ''[[RSPCA - Think Pig Campaign]]''\n[[Image:Pork Stir Fry ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|The ingredients]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 tablespoon [[Soy sauce|soy sauce]]\n| 2 teaspoons seasoned [[Rice vinegar|rice vinegar]] or [[White wine vinegar|white wine vinegar]]\n| 1 [[Juice|juice]] of 1 small [[Orange|orange]]\n| Grated [[zest]] of half an [[orange]]\n| 1 teaspoon dark [[Muscovado sugar|muscovado sugar]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Cornflour|cornflour]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]]\n| 85g unsalted [[Cashews|cashews]] [[Nuts|nuts]]\n| 4 to 6 [[Spring onions|spring onions]], sliced\n| 300g lean and thinly sliced [[Pork chops|pork chops]]\n| A selection of your favourite vegetables, eg:\n| 1 large [[Carrot|carrot]], cut into thin matchsticks\n| 150g pack [[mangetout]], sliced in half\n| 1 [[Red pepper|red pepper]], deseeded and thinly sliced\n}}\n'''to serve'''\n* 240g [[Plain boiled rice]] or [[noodles]]\n \n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix together the [[Soy sauce|soy sauce]], [[Vinegar|vinegar]], [[Orange juice|orange juice]], [[Muscovado sugar|muscovado sugar]] and [[Cornflour|cornflour]]. Set aside.\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a [[Wok|wok]]. Add the [[Cashews|cashews]] and cook for a minute until golden [[Brown|brown]]. Remove the [[Nuts|nuts]] and tip on to kitchen paper to drain. When cool enough to handle chop finely.\n| Add half of the [[Spring onion|spring onion]] and cook over a high heat for 3-5 minutes until just softened then lift them out and add to the [[Cashews|cashews]].\n| Add the [[Pork|pork]] and [[Carrots|carrots]] to the [[Wok|wok]] and [[Stir fry|stir fry]] for 3-4 minutes, add the [[Broccoli|broccoli]], [[Mange tout|mange tout]], [[Red pepper|red pepper]] and [[Cabbage|cabbage]] stir [[Fry|fry]] for another 4-5 minutes until the [[Vegetables|vegetables]] are tender yet still crunchy.\n| Stir the [[Cornflour|cornflour]] mixture to blend the ingredients, pour into the [[Wok|wok]] and [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] for a couple of minutes until the [[Sauce|sauce]] thickens. Stir in the [[Spring onion|spring onion]]. Serve the [[Stir fry|stir fry]] sprinkled with the [[Nuts|nuts]], the remaining [[spring onions]], set on a bed of [[Noodles|noodles]] or [[Rice|rice]].\n}}\n===Variations===\nCook the cashews in sesame oil, draining any excess into the soy sauce mix.\n===Chef's notes===\n{{Template:ThinkPig}} \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Stir fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#porkstirfry #nuts #cashews #wok #cornflour #pork #noodles #mangetout #muscovadosugar #orange #stirfry </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Prawn and cauliflower curry with lime and coconut",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Prawn and cauliflower curry with lime and coconut Indian recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#cauliflower #coffeegrinder #prawns #ground #garlic #noodles #nampla #bread #chillies #zest #simmer \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This simple Fishermans' curry from Vietnam has a wonderful spicy sauce and could be served with plain rice, noodles or even crusty bread\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3495\n|PortionCalories = 873\n|DatePublished=31st October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 45 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Prawn & cauliflower curry with lime and coconut recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Basil, more basil</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">The basil makes all the difference.  If you can get Thai basil, even better.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis simple Fishermans' curry from Vietnam has a wonderful spicy [[Sauce|sauce]] and could be served with [[Plain rice|plain rice]], [[Noodles|noodles]] or even crusty [[Bread|bread]].\n[[Image:Prawn & cauliflower curry ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|The ingredients]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 450 g (1 lb) raw tiger [[Prawns|prawns]], [[Scampi|scampi]], [[King prawns|king prawns]] etc.\n| [[Zest]] and [[Juice|juice]] of 1 [[Lime|lime]].\n| 1 tablespoon [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]].\n| 1 [[Onion|onion]], peeled and chopped.\n| 4 [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves, peeled and roughly chopped.\n| 4 [[Dried|dried]] birds' eye [[Chillies|chillies]], [[Ground|ground]] to powder in a [[Coffee grinder|coffee grinder]] or crushed in a [[Mortar and pestle|mortar and pestle]] (or to taste).\n| 1 [[Cauliflower|cauliflower]], broken into florets.\n| 1 teaspoon [[Jaggery|jaggery]] or [[Brown sugar|brown sugar]].\n| 1 teaspoon [[coriander seeds]], [[ground]] to a powder in a [[coffee grinder]].\n| 2 teaspoons [[fenugreek seeds]], ground to powder in a [[coffee grinder]].\n| 2 whole [[Star anise|star anise]], [[dry-fried]] and [[Ground|ground]] to a powder in a [[Coffee grinder|coffee grinder]].\n| 1 can (450ml) [[Coconut milk|coconut milk]].\n| A splash of [[nam pla]]\n| A handful of [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]] or [[basil leaves]], stalks removed, for garnish.\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]].\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Remove the shells from the [[Prawns|prawns]] and de-vein them. \n* Place in a bowl with the [[Lime|lime]] [[Zest|zest]] and juice and leave in a cool place for an hour or so if you have time.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Oil|oil]] to a hot [[Wok|wok]] and [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] the [[Onions|onions]] for 5 minutes, add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Chillies|chillies]] and as soon as the garlic starts to colour.\n| Add the [[Cauliflower|cauliflower]].\n| Add the [[Cauliflower|cauliflower]] and [[Stir-fry]] for 4 minutes, don't allow the [[Garlic|garlic]] to burn.\n| Add the [[Sugar|sugar]] and [[Spices|spices]], once combined, add the [[Coconut milk|coconut milk]] and the [[nam pla]].\n| Reduce to a low [[Simmer|simmer]] and heat for 10 to 15 minutes.\n| [[Simmer]] for a little longer if you feel it needs further reduction.\n| Add the bowl of [[Prawns|prawns]], together with the [[Lime juice|lime juice]] and cook until the prawns turn pink, this should only take 3 minutes or so.\n| Season to taste with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] and serve, sprinkled with [[Coriander|coriander]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe hot with [[Noodles|noodles]], [[Rice|rice]], or crusty [[Bread|bread]].\n===Variations===\nInstead of [[Cauliflower|cauliflower]], try [[Broccoli|broccoli]], cubes of [[Butternut squash|butternut squash]] or even [[Potatoes|potatoes]], though they will need par-[[Boiling|boiling]] first.\n===Chef's note===\nIf you prefer your cauliflower softer, then [[par boil]] it for 3 minutes before [[stir-frying]].\n'''This was a fantastic curry!'''  I made with one whole star anise (not one 'petal'), but I think it would be better with 2.  I used 6 dried [[birds' eye chillies]] and 2 large dried [[chile de Arbole]].  I had run out of limes so I used bottled lemon juice and a handful of crushed lemon leaves from our ornamental tree in the [[marinade]] and the cooking.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Vietnamese recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Indian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Stir fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#cauliflower #coffeegrinder #prawns #ground #garlic #noodles #nampla #bread #chillies #zest #simmer </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }

Serve with plain boiled rice\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1395\n|PortionCalories = 348\n|DatePublished=31st October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 2 hours 20 minutes\n |PrepTime = 2 hours 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 10 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Prawn stir-fry with French beans, galangal and garlic recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Beat this for a recipe!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.8</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">You can't!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Sue_spins|Susie]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Image:Prawn stir-fry with French beans, galangal and garlic.jpg|thumb|300px|right|..sauce reduced a little..]]\nA Vietnamese / Cambodian style dish that could work as well as a [[Starter|starter]] as it would for a [[Main course|main course]].  Serve with [[Plain boiled rice|plain boiled rice]]. If you cannot get [[Galangal|galangal]] then substitue [[Ginger|ginger]] instead.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 3 tablespoons [[Ghee|ghee]] or [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]]\n| 4 [[Garlic cloves, peeled and crushed|garlic cloves, peeled and crushed]]\n| 25 g [[Galangal|galangal]], (after peeling and [[Grating|grating]])\n| 450 g fresh [[Prawns|prawns]], peeled and deveined\n| 1 medium [[Onion|onion]], peeled and chopped finely\n| 450 g [[French beans]], topped and tailed\n| 120 ml [[Soy sauce|soy sauce]]\n}}\n'''[[Marinade]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 30 ml [[Fish sauce|fish sauce]] ([[Tuk trey|tuk trey]], [[Nuoc mam|nuoc mam]] or [[Nam pla|nam pla]])\n| [[Juice]] of two [[Limes|limes]] and [[Zest|zest]] of one\n| 10 ml (2 teaspoons) [[Jaggery|jaggery]] or [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| 2 [[Garlic cloves, peeled and crushed|garlic cloves, peeled and crushed]]\n| 1 [[Lemongrass]] stalk, sliced finely\n}}\n===Method===\n\n\n'''Marindade'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Fish sauce|fish sauce]], [[Lime juice|lime juice]] and [[Zest|zest]], [[Sugar|sugar]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Lemon grass|lemon grass]] and whisk until the sugar has dissolved\n| Add the [[Prawns|prawns]] to this [[Marinade|marinade]] and [[Refrigerate|refrigerate]] for 2 hours\n}}\n'''[[Beans]] and [[Prawns|prawns]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat 2 tablespoons of the [[Ghee|ghee]] in a [[Wok|wok]] and add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Galangal|galangal]]\n| Just as the [[Garlic|garlic]] starts to colour, add the [[Prawns|prawns]] and [[Marinade|marinade]]\n| [[Stir-fry]] until the [[Prawns|prawns]] turn pink\n| Tip the [[Prawns|prawns]] and [[Juice|juice]] into a bowl and reserve\n| Add the remaining tablespoons of [[Ghee|ghee]] and  [[Stir fry|stir fry]] the [[Onions|onions]] for 4 minutes until they colour\n| Add the [[Beans|beans]] and [[Soy sauce|soy sauce]] and cook for 4 minutes or until the [[Beans|beans]] are cooked to your liking\n| Turn up the heat and reduce the sauce if needed.\n| Tip the [[Prawn|prawn]] mixture back into the [[Wok|wok]] and heat for a minute or two\n| Serve immediately\n}}\n===Chef's note===\n[[Blanch]] the beans first for a few minutes in boiling water if you prefer them 'softer'.\n\nI am not keen on thin strips of [[lemon grass]] which can be a little tough unless it is really fresh, so I prefer to leave it whole. Just smash it with a cleaver to release the oils and then discard it when serving the meal.\n\nI made this for 2 but kept most of the quantities the same, apart from the soy sauce as 120ml seemed a lot.  I probably used 50ml.  It was delicious.  I may add more vegetables next time.\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Vietnamese recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Stir fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#prawns #prawnstirfrywithfrenchbeansgalangalandgarlic #galangal #marinade #beans #garlic #ghee #lemongrass #zest #wok #fishsauce </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

Any\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1029\n|PortionCalories = 514\n|DatePublished=5th June 2015\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Served with naan breads\n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  45 minutes\n|PrepTime =  20 minutes\n|CookTime =  25 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Seafood malai curry recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Nice spice mix</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">You cannot beat fresh spices in a curry. \ud83d\udc96</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nAn authentic Bengali [[Seafood|seafood]] [[Curry|curry]].  It could be made entirely with prawns but in this version I'm using a mixture of [[king prawns]] and [[cod fillet]]. Any white fish would do.\n\nThis is a fairly quick [[Curry|curry]], nice and creamy with lots of [[Coconut|coconut]] flavours.  As with all authentic [[Indian curries]] there are lots of whole [[Spices|spices]] that you are not supposed to eat.  Pick them out as you eat. You'll get a surprise if you bite down on a [[Cardamom|cardamom]] pod or a [[Clove|clove]]!\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 250g [8.5oz] mixture of large [[Prawns|prawns]] and any [[white fish]] cut into bite-sized pieces\n| &#189; teaspoon [[Ground|ground]] [[Turmeric|turmeric]]\n| Pinch of [[Salt|salt]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Ghee|ghee]], ([[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]] will be fine if you don't have ghee)\n| 1 fresh [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]]\n| 1 2.5 cm (1 inch) [[Cinnamon stick|cinnamon stick]]\n| 6 whole [[Cloves|cloves]]\n| 4 [[Green cardamom pods|green cardamom pods]]\n| 1 black [[Cardamom|cardamom]] pod\n| A few grates of [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]] using a microplane [[Grater|grater]]\n| 200 ml (half a can of full cream [[Coconut milk|coconut milk]]\n| 50g of creamed [[Coconut|coconut]] cut from a block\n| A tablespoon of [[dessicated coconut]]\n| 2 [[Indian green chillies]] [[Split|split]] lengthwise and deseeded\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Add the [[Seafood|seafood]] pieces to a [[Lock & Lock box]] together with the [[Turmeric|turmeric]] and [[Salt|salt]], close the ld and shake gently to coat evenly\n| Heat the [[Ghee|ghee]] in a [[Wok|wok]] or [[Frying pan|frying pan]], not too hot or you'll have a kitchen full of smoke\n| [[Stir-fry]] the [[Seafood|seafood]] for a few minutes turning often\n| Remove the cooked [[Seafood|seafood]], place in a clean bowl and set to one side\n| On a low heat in the same pan add all the [[Spices|spices]] apart from the [[Chillies|chillies]] and [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] for 2 or 3 minutes so the [[Ghee|ghee]] is nicely flavoured\n| Pour in the [[Coconut milk|coconut milk]] and add the [[Coconut block|coconut block]], cook for another few minutes\n| Add the [[Prawns|prawns]] and [[Chillies|chillies]], bring to a simmer then cook gently cook for 10 minutes\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Seafood malai curry ingredients.jpg|thumb|right|300px|The ingredient, less the seafood\nImage:Seafood malai curry frying prawns and fish.jpg|thumb|right|300px|Frying the prawns and cod pieces\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[Plain boiled rice|plain boiled rice]] and [[Naan breads|naan breads]]\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Indian recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy Because the [[beef]] is only cooked for a short time, it's worth using high quality beef such as fillet for this dish.\n[[Image:Seared beef and beanspouts with spicy lime dressing recipe.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Ingredients for seared [[beef]] and [[bean sprouts]] in a spicy lime dressing]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 450 g (1 lb) [[beef]] fillet steak, cut into 2.5 cm (1\") steaks\n| 115 g (4 oz) [[bean sprouts]]\n| 4 or 5 [[button mushrooms]]\n| Big handful of [[basil leaves]]\n| Big handful of [[mint leaves]]\n| 1 [[lime]], quartered for garnish\n| [[Peanut oil]] for [[frying]]\n| '''For the [[marinade]]'''\n| 2 [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves, crushed\n| [[Zest]] of 2 [[limes]]\n| Juice of 2 [[limes]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[nuoc mam]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[jaggery]]\n| 1 [[lemongrass]] stalk, bruised and chopped\n| 2 small hot [[red chillies]], deseeded and sliced into rings\n| 3 spring onions, [[sliced on the diagonal]]\n}}\n===Method===\n'''The [[marinade]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Whisk the [[lime juice]] and [[zest]], [[jaggery]] and [[nuoc mam]] until the [[jaggery]] dissolves\n| (if the [[jaggery]] is solid and hard, first crush it with the end of a rolling pin)\n| Mix in the crushed [[Garlic|garlic]], [[chillies]] and [[lemongrass]]\n}}\n\n'''The beef'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a hot pan with a little [[oil]], sear the fillets for 2 minutes per side, remove and allow to cool\n| Cut the [[meat]] into thin slices\n| Add to the [[marinade]] an refrigerate for at least 2 hours\n| Blanch the [[bean sprouts]] for 1 minutes in just [[boiled]] water. Allow to cool then arrange in a large serving bowl with the mint, basil and the chopped [[spring onions]].\n| After 2 hours, drain excess liquid from the [[meat]] and arrange in the bowl with the [[bean sprouts]]\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nGarnish with [[lime]] slices and serve with [[coconut rice]]\n===Chef's notes===\n\nI also added some raw sliced [[button mushrooms]] to the [[bean sprouts]] because I happened to have some left over.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Beef]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine|Beef]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Indian recipes|Beef]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Beef]]\n[[Category:Marinades dressings and butters|Beef]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Beef]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes|Beef]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Beef]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Indonesian recipes|Beef]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#beansprouts #jaggery #beef #marinade #limes #zest #lemongrass #lime #garlic #nuocmam #buttonmushrooms </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

''[[Roasted sweet peppers|see here for a how-to but with sweet peppers]]''\n| Remove the seeds and slice thinly into a bowl\n| Peel the [[grapefruit]] and cut into segments, removing as much pith as possible, add to the bowl\n| Cut the [[onion]] into very thin rings, add to the bowl\n| Chill for 30 minutes\n| Oil 4 sheets of [[tin foil]] (so the [[fish]] does not stick to it)\n| Sprinkle half of the [[ginger]] and [[spring onions]] on the foil\n| Season the [[bass]] with [[salt]] and [[freshly ground black pepper]]\n| Lay the fish on the [[ginger]] and [[spring onions]], then sprinkle the remaining [[ginger]] and [[spring onions]] over the top\n| Wrap the fish so you have four individual parcels\n| Place the parcels in the [[steamer]] over a pan of [[boiling]] water\n| [[Steam]] for 8 minutes\n| Discard the [[ginger]] and [[spring onions]]\n| Garnish with [[coriander]] and serve with the salsa\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe hot with [[peas and peppers]]\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Bass]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes|Bass]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine|Bass]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes|Bass]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Bass]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Bass]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Student recipes|Bass]]\n[[Category:Steamed]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#springonions #seabasswithgrapefruitsalsa #ginger #grapefruit #chillies #coriander #peasandpeppers #seabass #onion #steam #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Sesame prawn fritters",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Sesame prawn fritters recipe Accompaniments\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#sesameprawnfritters #sesameseeds #miseenplace #drysherry #deepfried #unusualrecipes #cornflour #whitefish #bones #sesameoil #fritter \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=I tried to attempt a healthier variation of the deep fried the prawn ball recipe in the form of a fritter. It works pretty well I feel\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 581\n|PortionCalories = 290\n|DatePublished=23rd October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 2 to 4 with a selection of other starters\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 30 minutes\n|PrepTime = 15 minutes\n|CookTime = 15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Sesame prawn fritters.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Golden crunchies</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">A nice change and healthy, not being deep fried.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nI tried to attempt a healthier variation of the deep fried the prawn ball recipe in the form of a [[Fritter|fritter]]. It works pretty well I feel.\n[[Image:RecipeSesame prawn fritters.jpg|thumb|right|300px|Sesame prawn fritters - shallow fried]]\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 6 oz (150g) any [[white fish]]\n| 4 oz (100g) peeled prawns\n| 1 egg white\n| 1 heaped tablespoon of [[cornflour]]\n| 1 tablespoon rice wine or [[dry sherry]]\n| 1.5 tablespoons [[sesame oil]]\n| 3 tablespoons [[sesame seeds]] \n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the oven to 220C/425F/gas 7\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Remove any skin and [[bones]] from the fish\n| Mince or finely chop the prawns\n| Mix the prawns and fish together well, then add the remaining ingredients apart from the sesame seeds.\n| Mix very well\n| Shape into flat discs (about the size of a jam-pot lid)\n| Coat with [[sesame seeds]]\n| Place on a lightly oiled tray the top of the oven for 10-15 minutes or until golden brown\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nServe hot with a dip such as [[Sweet and sour sauce|sweet and sour sauce]], [[Sesame and hoisin dip|sesame and hoisin dip]],[[Tomato_and_chili_dip|tomato and chili dip]] or [[Peanut sauce|peanut sauce]] and slivers of fresh red chillies.\n\n===Chef's note===\n\nThese could of course be [[shallow fried]] or even [[deep fried]], this was just a healthy experiment.  They come out quite nice, though not as golden as they would if they were fried.\n===Variations===\nMade this again recently and added lots of chopped [[parsley]] and a tablespoon or so of [[masa harina]] to bind the mixture and add a slightly different flavour.\n==See also==\n{{FritterRecipes}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Prawns]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Prawns]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine|Prawns]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes|Prawns]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes|Prawn]]\n[[Category:Starters|Prawns]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Prawns]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#sesameprawnfritters #sesameseeds #miseenplace #drysherry #deepfried #unusualrecipes #cornflour #whitefish #bones #sesameoil #fritter </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

The only problem is that they are not very good for you if you are watching your [[cholesterol]] intake.  Anything that contains [[Lard|lard]] and is then fried, can't be great for you. Anyway, it's probably worth being naughty now and again.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 slices of processed white [[Bread|bread]]\n| 85 g (3 oz) [[Sesame seeds|sesame seeds]]\n| 55 g (2 oz) [[Pork|pork]] [[Fat|fat]] or 2 tablespoons [[Lard|lard]] or white [[Cooking fat|cooking fat]]\n| 100 g (4 oz) [[Peeled prawns|peeled prawns]]\n| 1 [[Egg white|egg white]]\n| 3 teaspoons [[Cornflour|cornflour]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]] to taste\n| [[Oil]] for [[Frying|frying]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Very finely chop the pork fat and the [[Prawns|prawns]]\n| Whisk the [[Egg white|egg white]] and mix with [[Salt|salt]], [[Pepper|pepper]] and the [[Cornflour|cornflour]] and blend this into the [[Prawns|prawns]]\n| Spread this paste on to one side of the [[Bread|bread]] leaving a gap around the edge.\n| Shake the [[Sesame seeds|sesame seeds]] on to a saucer and press the paste side of the [[Bread|bread]] into the seeds to take on a thick layer of seeds\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a deep pan until a small cube of [[Bread|bread]] sizzles and browns when dropped into the oil\n| Carefully lower each slice of [[Bread|bread]] into the [[Oil|oil]], spread-side down and [[Fry|fry]] for 3 minutes, turn over and fry for a further minute.\n| Remove and drain on absorbent paper.\n| Cut off the crusts and slice the toasts into strips\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nServe immediately with a selection of dips. Shoyu being Japanese soy sauce, derived from wheat, not soya beans\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 307\n|PortionCalories = 153\n|DatePublished=1st January 2015\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Beef Shoyu Ramen Hajime from [http://www.eshtravaganza.com/hajime-ramen-pik-the-first-steak-ramen-in-indonesia/ Hajime Ramen Pik - Indonesia]\n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  1 hour, 15 minutes\n|PrepTime =  1 hour, 10 minutes\n|CookTime =  5 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Shoyu beef recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Nice change</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">A nice light flavour this one. And the sichuan [[Peppercorn|peppercorn]] is largely responsible for that. I just love the tingly, numbing, citrusy, sharp taste.''\n\n''So I was delighted to discover this homemade [[Chili oil|chili oil]]. To me, it's simply Sichuan in a Bottle.\"''\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 6 tablespoons [[Sichuan peppercorns|sichuan peppercorns]] (pictured)\n| 8 tablespoons [[Chili flakes|chili flakes]] (ready bought or chop some [[Dried chillies|dried chillies]] yourself)\n| 1 teaspoon [[Salt|salt]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Sesame oil|sesame oil]]\n| 360 ml [[Peanut oil|peanut oil]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Put everything except the [[Oil|oil]] in a heat proof container.\n| Heat [[Oil|oil]] between 107 to 122.5 [[Degrees|degrees]] [[Celsius]] and pour over the other ingredients. Be careful because it will sizzle. (Or actually, when you have a [[Thermometer|thermometer]], like I do, you will notice it won't sizzle at all. If you don't, then yes, be careful)\n| Leave to cool down. After the flavours have blended for a day you can [[Sieve|sieve]] the [[Oil|oil]], if you wish. \n|Store in your [[Refrigerator|refrigerator]] for a couple of weeks.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Szechuan chilli oil - heated.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Heating the chillies and peppercorns\nImage:Szechuan chilli oil - cold.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Opaque when taken from the fridge\n</gallery>\n===Robin's notes===\nFunny thing is that with my version it always \u201csets\u201d.\n\nWhen I take it out of the fridge it will become nice and translucent again, but cold it looks like this.\n\nI\u2019m quite sure it doesn\u2019t make any difference to the taste, but if anybody knows why this happens, please tell me! (*edit* It\u2019s the type of oil) \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:FotoosVanRobin recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#sichuanpeppercorns #sichuanchilioil #chinesecuisine #peanutoil #celsius #sesameoil #sieve #thermometer #degrees #refrigerator #chiliflakes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

If you don't have spring onions, use normal onions, sliced.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 [[sea bass]] fillets\n| 7.5 cm (3\") [[ginger root]], peeled and [[julienned]]\n| 4 [[spring onions]] [[sliced on the diagonal]]\n| Fresh [[coriander]] to garnish\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Oil 4 sheets of [[tin foil]] (so the fish does not stick to it)\n| Sprinkle half of the [[ginger]] and [[spring onions]] on the foil\n| Season the bass with [[salt]] and [[freshly ground black pepper]]\n| Lay the fish on the [[ginger]] and [[spring onions]], then sprinkle the remaining [[ginger]] and [[spring onions]] over the top\n| Wrap the fish loosely so you have four individual parcels\n| Place the parcels in the [[steamer]] over a pan of [[boiling]] water\n| [[Steam]] for 8 minutes\n| Discard the [[ginger]] and [[spring onions]]\n| Garnish with [[coriander]] and serve with the [[salsa]]\n}}\n===Variations===\n\nInclude various herbs in the foil parcel such as fennel, parsley or dill.  Discard them before serving and add a sprinkle of the same herbs, but fresh, not soggy.\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Bass]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine|Bass]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes|Bass]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Freshwater fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Bass]]\n[[Category:Student recipes]]\n[[Category:Steamed]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#springonions #ginger #simplesteamedfish #coriander #tinfoil #steam #julienned #gingerroot #salsa #seabass #steamed </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

It should be quite spicy, though you can temper the heat by varying the amount of\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1735\n|PortionCalories = 867\n|DatePublished=31st October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 2\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 20 minutes\n |PrepTime = 5 minutes\n |CookTime = 15 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Singapore noodles recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Buy those beansprout!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">This is fabulous food</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis recipe is quick and simple to cook and makes a complete meal.\n\nIt should be quite spicy, though you can temper the heat by varying the amount of [[Chillies|chillies]] used.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 125 g [[Dried|dried]] [[Egg noodles|egg noodles]]\n| 14 large [[King prawns|king prawns]] or about 100g - properly [[defrosted]] if [[Frozen|frozen]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Oil|oil]] - I use [[Olive oil|olive oil]] but to be more authentic, use [[Groundnut oil|groundnut oil]]\n| 2 Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and crushed - or to taste\n| 2.5 cm piece of [[Ginger|ginger]], peeled and [[Julienned|julienned]]\n| 1 medium [[Red onion|red onion]], peeled and sliced\n| 1 [[Sweet pepper|sweet pepper]], deseeded and sliced\n| 50 g [[Bacon|bacon]] [[Lardons|lardons]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Curry paste|curry paste]] (or [[Curry powder|curry powder]])\n| 1 hot green [[Chili]], finely chopped (or to taste)\n| 150 g [[Beansprouts|beansprouts]]\n| 3 tablespoons of [[Dark soy sauce|dark soy sauce]]\n}}\n'''to garnish'''\n* a few [[Roasted|roasted]] [[Nuts|nuts]] of your choice\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Cook the [[Noodles|noodles]] in a large pan of [[Boiling|boiling]] water for 4 to 5 minutes - leave in a [[Sieve|sieve]] to drain\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a hot [[Wok|wok]] and saut\u00e9 the [[Ginger|ginger]], [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Chillies|chillies]] for 2 or 3 minutes\n| Add the [[Onions|onions]] and [[Pepper|pepper]], reduce the heat a little and cook until the onions start to become translucent\n| Add the [[Bacon|bacon]] on cook for a minute, then add the [[Prawns|prawns]]\n| Once the [[Prawns|prawns]] have turned pink add the remaining ingredients and the cooked [[Noodles|noodles]]\n| [[Stir-fry]] for a minute or two, mixing well\n| Serve immediately, garnished with [[Roasted|roasted]] [[Nuts|nuts]]\n}}\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n===See also===\n* [[Air fried Singapore noodles with chicken, courgettes and mushrooms]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Vietnamese recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Shellfish recipes]]\n[[Category:Stir fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#singaporenoodles #garlic #bacon #chillies #prawns #noodles #ginger #nuts #roasted #dried #unusualrecipes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Sous vide hoisin duck breasts",

                    {

                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Sous vide hoisin sauce duck breast recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#duck #sear #sousvidehoisinduckbreasts #toastedsesameseeds #sesameoil #hoisinsauce #blackricevinegar #wok #stirfry #slowcooker #sousvidecooking \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=The most tender duck breasts you will ever taste, cooked sous vide.  Temperatures and times with photographs\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n==Sous vide hoisin duck breasts==\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1143\n|PortionCalories = 571\n|DatePublished=4th February 2015\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 2 hours 15 minutes\n|PrepTime = 10 minutes\n|CookTime = 2 hours 5 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Sous vide hoisin duck breasts recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Noodles and hoisin!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Yummily.  This was very special.  Try it!!!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nFlushed with the absolute success cooking [[Lamb chops|lamb chops]] in my homemade sous vide [[Slow cooker|slow cooker]] conversion kit, I think [[Duck|duck]] is next.\n\nThis time I wanted to add some flavours to the vacuum sealed pouches and as [[Hoisin|hoisin]] works so well with [[Duck|duck]], I thought I would try that.  I also added a teaspoon of Chinkiang black vice [[Vinegar|vinegar]] as I love its subtle flavour and in may [[Tenderise|tenderise]] the duck a little too.  It is likely that most of the vinegar is likely to be sucked out of the pouch during the vacuum process, so to this end I used enough plastic to make a pouch that would hang over the edge of the counter top whilst sealing, hopefully to lessen the effect.\n\nThis was a superb meal.  The duck breast was so tender you could have pushed your finger through it.  It had the flavour and mouthfeel of a rare duck breast, without all that blood.  Marvellous!\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 310g [[Duck|duck]] breasts, skin on [2]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Hoisin sauce|hoisin sauce]]\n| 2 teaspoons Chinkiang [[Black rice vinegar|black rice vinegar]]\n}}\n''' to serve'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 packet prepared [[Stir fry|stir fry]] mix.  Yes, I know it's [[Cheating|cheating]], but it is a weekday!\n| 160g [[Egg noodles|egg noodles]] (about 2 'nests')\n| 1 tablespoon [[Toasted sesame seeds|toasted sesame seeds]]\n| [[Sesame oil|sesame oil]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* If you are luck enough to have a [[Jaccard meat tenderiser]], stamp the breast all over on the skin side to puncture the skin and provide a path for the flavours to penetrate the [[Meat|meat]].\n* Make up 2 vacuum pouches that will be large enough to [[Hand|hand]] over the counter top while the breasts are being sealed.\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Browning the duck breasts.jpg|Browning the duck breasts on both sides\nImage:Hang the duck breast pouches over the worktop.jpg|Hang the pouches over the worktop to try to prevent sucking all of the marinade out of the pouch\nImage:Duck breasts Jaccard meat tenderizer.jpg|Stamp the duck breasts with the Jaccard meat tenderiser\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Place a teaspoon of [[Hoisin sauce|hoisin sauce]] and a teaspoon of Chinkiang [[Black rice vinegar|black rice vinegar]] in each pouch \n| Pop a [[Duck|duck]] breast in each pouch and wipe the inside of the pouch where it will be sealed with a [[Paper towel|paper towel]].\n| Hang the pouch over the edge of the countertop and [[Vacuum seal|vacuum seal]].\n| Set your sous vide bath to 56.5\u00b0C (''133.7\u00b0F'')\n| Suspend the pouches in the bath and heat for 2 hours\n| When the [[Duck|duck]] breasts have cooked, get a heavy based [[Frying pan|frying pan]] very hot with no [[Oil|oil]] and [[Sear|sear]] the duck breasts, skin side down for 2 minutes\n| If you have a mapp [[Blowtorch|blow torch]] you can [[Sear|sear]] the [[Meat|meat]] side of the breast while the skin is being crisped.  I wouldn't bother with a propane blowtorch unless you like the taste of propane fuel.\n| Meanwhile cook your [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] mix in a hot [[Wok|wok]] with a little [[Oil|oil]] and pop the [[Noodle|noodle]] nests in [[Boiling|boiling]] water for 4 minutes.\n| Drain and toss in [[Sesame oil|sesame oil]] and a teaspoon of [[Toasted sesame seeds|toasted sesame seeds]].\n| Slice the [[Duck|duck]] breasts diagonally into bite-size pieces and serve.\n}}\n{{SousVideSeeAlso}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Thai recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Sous vide recipes]]\n[[Category:Sous vide cooking]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#duck #sear #sousvidehoisinduckbreasts #toastedsesameseeds #sesameoil #hoisinsauce #blackricevinegar #wok #stirfry #slowcooker #sousvidecooking </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Spicy chicken with coconut and cardamom",
                "revisions": [
                    {

However, once cooked it just imparts a warm flavour, nothing like the smell of a Gym!\n\nThis needs to be prepared a day in advance for the [[Marinade|marinade]] to penetrate the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n}}\n'''cooking the [[Chicken|chicken]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1.6 kg (3.5 lb) [[Chicken drumsticks|chicken drumsticks]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Sunflower oil|sunflower oil]]\n| A grind of [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| 400ml can [[Coconut milk|coconut milk]]\n| 4 large [[Green chillies|green chillies]] de-seeded and finely chopped into rings\n}}\n'''the [[Marinade|marinade]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 teaspoon [[Turmeric powder|turmeric powder]]\n| 1 [[Scant|scant]] tablespoon [[Cardamom pods|cardamom pods]] in their shells ([[Brown|brown]] and/or green)\n| 1 tablespoon [[Crushed garlic|crushed garlic]]\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Ginger root|ginger root]], peeled and [[Grated|grated]] (use any [[Juice|juice]] too!)\n| 2 [[Green Indian chillies|green indian chillies]], deseeded and thinly sliced\n| 1 teaspoon freshly [[Ground cumin seeds|ground cumin seeds]]\n| 1 teaspoon freshly [[Ground coriander|ground coriander]] seeds\n| 80 ml plain [[Natural yogurt|natural yogurt]]\n| [[Zest]] and [[Juice|juice]] of one [[Lime|lime]]\n}}\n'''to serve'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| Chopped [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]]\n| 20 ml [[Yogurt|yogurt]] drizzled over the dish\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Chicken marinade.jpg|thumb|300px|right|After 30 seconds of shaking!\nImage:Chicken marinade ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Marinade ingredients, ready to mix.\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Remove the skin from the [[Chicken drumsticks|chicken drumsticks]].\n| Cut 3 or 4 deep slashes, right down to the bone of the [[Drumsticks|drumsticks]] so the [[Marinade|marinade]] can penetrate the flesh.\n| Add the [[Chicken drumsticks|chicken drumsticks]] to a large [[Lock and Lock box]].\n| Using a [[Pestle and mortar|pestle and mortar]], crush the shells of the [[Cardamom pods|cardamom pods]] to release the [[Seeds|seeds]].  Discard the shells.\n| Crush the [[Cardamom seeds|cardamom seeds]] in the [[Pestle and mortar|pestle and mortar]] and add to the [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces.\n| Add the remaining [[Marinade|marinade]] ingredients to the [[Lock and Lock box|lock and lock box]], close the lid and shake violently for 30 seconds.  That's the mixing done!\n| Leave in a cool place overnight to [[Marinate|marinate]], shaking now and then.\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a [[Wok|wok]] or large pan and add a good grind of [[Black pepper|black pepper]]\n| Remove the [[Chicken|chicken]] and set the [[Marinade|marinade]] to one side.\n| Gently [[Brown|brown]] the [[Chicken|chicken]] all over.\n| Add the [[Coconut milk|coconut milk]] and the reserve [[Marinade|marinade]] and ring to the [[Boil|boil]].\n| [[Simmer]] for 35 minutes.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with chopped [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]] and a drizzle of [[Yogurt|yogurt]], accompanied by [[Plain rice|plain rice]]\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Indian recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Stir fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#marinade #chicken #chickendrumsticks #spicychickenwithcoconutandcardamom #coconutmilk #cardamompods #corianderleaves #pestleandmortar #blackpepper #juice #yogurt </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }

(for two)\n|Servings = Serves 4 to 6\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 50 minutes\n|PrepTime = 30 minutes\n|CookTime = 20 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Spicy Chinese cabbage.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">That wok looks very well used</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">It also looks very authentic</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Sue_spins|Susie]] </span></span>\n}}\nA simple spicy vegetable dish that could be served on it's own or as an accompaniment.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 900g (2lb) [[Chinese leaves]] ([[Brassica rapa]], [[Bok choy]], [[Siew choy]], etc)\n| 3 tablespoons [[dark soy sauce]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[sugar]]\n| 1 teaspoon sea [[salt]]\n| 3 tablespoons Chinese rice wine or [[dry sherry]]\n| 6 teaspoons [[vegetable stock]]\n| 1 fresh [[red chilli]] or to taste\n| 2 [[spring onions]] (scallions)\n| 5 fresh [[Shiitake mushrooms]] or\n| 5 dried [[Chinese mushrooms]]\n| 4 tablespoons vegetable oil\n| 1 tablespoon toasted [[sesame seeds]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| If using [[dried mushrooms]], fill a bowl with boiling water and soak them for 30 minutes\n| Slice the mushrooms thinly\n| Cut the [[cabbage]] into 1.5\" pieces, wash and drain\n| Chop [[spring onions]] into &#189;\" pieces - [[on the diagonal]]\n| Finely slice the chillies, removing the seeds if you don't want it too hot\n| Mix together the dark soy, sugar, [[salt]], [[wine]] and [[stock]]\n| Heat the oil in a wok as you would for frying [[onions]], add [[chillies]] and [[spring onions]] and [[stir-fry]] for 2 minutes\n| Add [[cabbage]] and [[mushrooms]], reduce the heat a little and stir-fry for 5 minutes\n| Add the [[soy sauce]] mixture and simmer uncovered for 10 minutes\n| If the liquid has not reduced, you can pour some of the excess away - as happened when I made this for two people.\n| Place in a serving bowl and sprinkle with the toasted [[sesame seeds]]\n| Serve immediately\n}}\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Cabbage]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes|Cabbage]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine|Cabbage]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Cabbage]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Cabbage]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Cabbage]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Stir fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#spicychinesecabbage #springonions #cabbage #sesameseeds #siewchoy #driedmushrooms #mushrooms #bokchoy #redchilli #darksoysauce #onions </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Varoma / Speed 1'''.\n| Afterwards, add the [[Soya sauce|soya sauce]], [[Vinegar|vinegar]], [[Cumin|cumin]] and the [[Sugar|sugar]] and program '''10 minutes / 100\u00b0 / Speed 2'''.\n| Once finished, add the [[Coriander|coriander]] and a pinch of [[Salt|salt]] and [[Blend|blend]] '''10 seconds / Speed 5'''.\n| Allow to cool and transfer into airtight jars.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nThis [[Sauce|sauce]] can be served cold or hot.  It is an ideal [[Accompaniment|accompaniment]] to oriental dishes and all types of [[Roast|roast]] [[Meats|meats]].  \n===Chef's notes===\nIt is very spicy and therefore it is recommended that it be served in moderation.  It is advisable to wear gloves when handling the guindillas and avoid contact with the eyes.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Thermomix recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#tomato #coriander #garlic #soyasauce #thermomix #oliveoil #redpeppers #meats #thermomixrecipes #peppers #ricevinegar </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

the colour is from the wine and tomato puree]]\n\nIt's a slight variation on the [[Chinese pork spare ribs|Chinese pork spare rib]] recipe.\n\nThe marinade looks far too liquid when it's made, but it eventually turns into a nice sticky, tasty coating at the end of the cooking process\n\n\n'''The ribs'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1.4 kg (3 lb) [[Pork spare ribs|pork spare ribs]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]]\n}}\n'''The sauce'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 3 [[Cloves garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves garlic, peeled and crushed]] with 1 teaspoon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 275 ml (10 fl oz) [[Red wine|red wine]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Worcestershire sauce]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Sherry vinegar|sherry vinegar]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Tomato puree|tomato puree]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Chili powder|chili powder]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Mustard powder|mustard powder]]\n| 1 tablespoon runny [[Honey|honey]]\n| 2 teaspoons freshly [[Grated|grated]] [[Ginger|ginger]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Ground ginger powder|ground ginger powder]]\n| [[Freshly ground black pepper]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the oven to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - Gas 4)\n===Method===\n\n\n''' The [[Sauce|sauce]]'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add all the [[Sauce|sauce]] ingredients to a bowl and whisk into a smooth sauce\n| Don't worry, it's quite a liquid mix\n| Place the ribs in a deep dish and pour the marinade over them , leave in a cool place for a few hours if you can\n}}\n'''The ribs'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Spread the ribs out on a deep [[Oil|oil]]ed [[baking tray]]\n| Place the ribs on the baking tray and baste with the marinade. A cookery [[Brush|brush]] is good for this\n| Put them on the top shelf of the oven and [[Roast|roast]] for 45 minutes\n| After 45 minutes, pull them out and re-[[Baste|baste]] them; cook for a further 10 to 25 minutes. They'll be safely cooked after 45 minutes, you're now just waiting for the sauce to cook down and thicken up.  Remove them once they are done to your satisfaction.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe hot with a nice [[:Category:Rice recipes|rice dish]] and a [[tomato and onion salad]]\n===Variations===\nKeeps the liquid and honey content roughly as the recipe and adjust the spices to suit your taste.\n===Chef's tip===\nA honey tip from [[User:JuliaBalbilla]].  If you only have normal honey, pop it in the microwave for a few seconds to convert.\n\nTo save a little time on the washing-up, use [[Bake-O-Glide]].\n\n{{Template:ThinkPig}}\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Spare ribs]]\n[[Category:Barbecue recipes|Spare ribs]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes|Spare]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine|Spare ribs]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes|Spare ribs]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Spare ribs]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Spare ribs]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes|Spare ribs]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Spare ribs]]\n[[Category:Starters|Spare ribs]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Marinaded]][[Category:Grilled, griddled or barbecued]][[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#spicyporkspareribs #porkspareribs #sauce #chilipowder #redwine #brush #bakingtray #tomatopuree #ginger #baste #roast </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

It will\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2724\n|PortionCalories = 272\n|DatePublished=17th January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Servings: 10 - Makes 250 ml (8 fl oz)\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 15 minutes plus cooling time\n|PrepTime = 2 minutes\n|CookTime = 13 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Dill oil recipe recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">This is unusual</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">And very tasty.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis Vietnamese condiment is great with [[noodles]] and [[soups]] and is a brilliant way to use up the glut from the garden before they go to seed.\n\nIt will keep for 2 weeks if sealed and refrigerated\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 250 ml (8 fl oz) [[groundnut oil]] or [[vegetable oil]]  ([[olive oil]] would be healthier, but not authentic)\n| 16 [[spring onions]],washed, trimmed and very finely sliced on the diagonal\n| 2.5 cm (1\") [[ginger root]], peeled and sliced\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[oil]] in a pan and add the [[ginger]] and [[spring onions]]\n| [[Fry]] for about 10 to 15 minutes until the [[spring onions]] turn golden\n| Keep the heat on the low side to ensure you don't burn the ingredients as this may bring out unpleasant flavours.\n| Allow to cool fully and then strain or sieve out all the solids\n| Store in sealed jars in the [[fridge]]\n}}\n{{Template:PeelingGinger}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Vietnamese tablespoon [[Cornflour|cornflour]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n'''If the [[Asparagus|asparagus]] are really tough:'''\n# Use a [[Speed peeler|speed peeler]] to strip any thick skin.\n# [[Blanch|blanch]] them for a few minutes in [[Boiling|boiling]] water.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]], add the [[Asparagus|asparagus]] slices and [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] for 4 minutes.\n| Mix the [[Cornflour|cornflour]] with a tablespoon of cold water and set aside.\n| Add the [[Ginger|ginger]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Stir fry|stir fry]] for a minute or until the garlic starts to colour.\n| Add the [[Sugar|sugar]], [[Vinegar|vinegar]], [[Wine|wine]] or [[Sherry|sherry]], [[Soy sauce|soy sauce]], [[lemon juice]] and [[Salt|salt]] and heat for 2 minutes.\n| Add the [[Cornflour|cornflour]] mix, [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] for 1 minute and serve.\n}}\n{{Template:Belazu attribution}}\n==See also==\n* [[Sweet and sour Absolutely gorgeous!\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1674\n|PortionCalories = 418\n|DatePublished=31st October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Sweet and sour chicken livers recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">It's very different!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.8</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">An unusual way to serve liver, the addition of pineapple makes this fabulously fruity.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n\n}}\n\nA economical and tasty Chinese dish for those who love the combination of [[Offal|offal]] and [[Fruit|fruit]]!  Absolutely gorgeous!\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 tablespoons [[Groundnut oil|groundnut oil]]\n| 450 g (1 lb) [[Chicken livers]], rinsed, dried, trimmed and cut into bite-sized pieces.\n| 4 to 6 tablespoons of [[yellow cornmeal]].\n| 2 [[bell peppers|green bell peppers]], de-seeded and cut into chunks.\n| 4 slices of canned [[Pineapple|pineapple]] rings cut into chunks.\n| 4 tablespoons [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]].\n}}\n'''Sweet and sour sauce'''\n* 2 tablespoons [[Cornflour|cornflour]].\n* 100g (4 oz) [[White sugar|white sugar]].\n* 2 tablespoons [[Light soy sauce|light soy sauce]].\n* 120 ml (4 fl oz) [[White wine vinegar|white wine vinegar]].\n* 120 ml (4 fl oz) water.\n\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[cornmeal]] to a plate and roll the chicken livers around so they are well coated.\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] and [[Fry|fry]] the [[Chicken livers|chicken livers]] in batches until they are nicely [[Browned|browned]].  Set aside and keep warm.\n| Add the [[Peppers|peppers]] to the [[Wok|wok]] and [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] for 4 minutes on a very high heat so they brown up a little.\n| Add the [[Stock|stock]] and the [[Pineapple|pineapple]] chunks, bring to the [[Boil|boil]], cover and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 4 minutes.\n| Mix the cornflour to a paste with a little of the water. Add to the remaining sweet and sour sauce ingredients and stir into the [[Wok|wok]], heat and allow to thicken.  It will turn all of a sudden. Once it has thickened, mix well and remove from the heat.\n| Pour the [[Sauce|sauce]] over the [[Chicken livers|chicken livers]].\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Sweet and sour chicken livers cornflour.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Thickened by the cornflour\nImage:Sweet and sour peppers.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Peppers browned, simmering in stock\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe immediately with [[Plain boiled rice|plain boiled rice]].\n===variations===\nThe Chilli-heads amongst you, may like to add some [[Tabasco sauce]] or [[chilli oil]] to this just before serving.\n===Chef's note===\nDon't be alarmed by the quantity and liquidity of the sweet and sour sauce before it is cooked.  It will thicken up once cooked.\n\nI find that rolling the [[chicken livers]] in [[yellow cornmeal]] gives an nice crunchy texture, though it's probably not very authentic.\n==See also==\n* [[Sweet and sour recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Offal recipes]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Stir fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#sweetandsourchickenlivers #chickenlivers #yellowcornmeal #pineapple #wok #cornmeal #lightsoysauce #fry #bellpeppers #cornflour #fruit </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Add the [[Lime juice|lime juice]] and [[Zest|zest]] and [[Salt|salt]] to taste.\n| Mix in the [[Chillies|chillies]], [[Shallots|shallots]], mints and [[Cucumbers|cucumbers]] with the dressing and [[Refrigerate|refrigerate]] for 20 minutes.\n| Mix well before serving.\n}}\n==See also==\n* [[Sweet and sour recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chinese recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Vietnamese recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#cucumber #sweetandsourcucumbersaladwithmintandchillies #zest #shallots #cucumbers #mintleaves #greenchillies #juice #whitesugar #papertowel #whitewinevinegar </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Do give it a try\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1397\n|PortionCalories = 349\n|DatePublished=23rd October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 35 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 20 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Sweet and sour pork recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Nice and sticky</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Not too sweet and quite tangy</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:NonLoggedInUser|NonLoggedInUser]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis favourite Chinese meal is fairly simple to make.  Do give it a try.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| '''For the [[batter]]'''\n| 1 tablespoon (15 ml) [[Rice wine|rice wine]] or [[Dry sherry|dry sherry]]\n| 1 tablespoon (15 ml) [[Peanut oil|peanut oil]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Curry powder|curry powder]]\n| 1 [[Egg|egg]], beaten\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| '''for the [[Sauce|sauce]]'''\n| 450g (1 lb) lean [[Pork|pork]] such as [[Pork fillet|pork fillet]], cubed\n| 1 [[Clove|clove]] of [[Garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| 2 teaspoons (10 ml) [[Peanut oil|peanut oil]]\n| &#189; [[Green bell pepper|green bell pepper]], deseeded and chopped into cubes\n| &#189; [[Red bell pepper|red bell pepper]], deseeded and chopped into cubes\n| 1 small [[Onion|onion]], peeled and roughly chopped (optional)\n| 100 g (4 oz) [[Cornflour|cornflour]]\n| 75 g (3 oz) [[Sugar|sugar]]\n| 50 g (2 oz) [[Tomato ketchup|tomato ketchup]]\n| 1 teaspoon (5 ml) [[Sesame oil|sesame oil]]\n| 1 teaspoon (5 ml) [[White wine vinegar|white wine vinegar]]\n| [[Oil]] for [[Deep-frying|deep-frying]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a bowl, make a [[batter]] by whisking the [[Sherry|sherry]] (or [[Wine|wine]]), [[Oil|oil]], [[Curry powder|curry powder]], beaten [[Egg|egg]], [[Cornflour|cornflour]] and a pinch of [[Salt|salt]]\n| Drop the cubed [[Pork|pork]] into the [[batter]] and coat well\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] for [[Deep-frying|deep-frying]] until it is [[Smoking|smoking]] and then add the [[Pork|pork]] cubes a few at a time, [[Fry|fry]] for 3 minutes, remove, drain on kitchen paper and set aside.\n| Reheat the [[Oil|oil]] and [[Fry|fry]] the cubes again, a few at a time, for 2 minutes each\n| Drain and reserve\n| In a [[Wok|wok]], heat 2 teaspoons of [[Peanut oil|peanut oil]] and fry the [[Peppers|peppers]] for 3 minutes.  [[Fry]] the [[Onion|onion]] with the peppers if using\n| Add the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Sugar|sugar]], [[Tomato ketchup|tomato ketchup]] and [[Wine vinegar|wine vinegar]] until the [[Sugar|sugar]] has dissolved\n| Bring to the [[Boil|boil]], add the [[Pork|pork]] cubes\n| Stir in the [[Sesame oil|sesame oil]] and serve\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe hot with [[Plain boiled rice|plain boiled rice]]\n===Variations===\nAdd [[Toasted|toasted]] (unsalted) [[Cashew nuts|cashew nuts]] at the final stage when adding the [[Sesame oil|sesame oil]]\n===Chef's notes===\n{{Template:ThinkPig}}\n==See also==\n* [[Sweet and sour recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Cooking with wine]]\n[[Category:Deep fried]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pork #batter #sesameoil #peanutoil #fry #sweetandsourpork #cornflour #egg #garlic #onion #tomatoketchup </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
